    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_14 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_14 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_14 * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_3.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;

float u_xlat7;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;

    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat7);

    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;

    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;

    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;

    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat4.y;

    u_xlat16_2.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_2.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BumpMapNr2_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in mediump vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in mediump vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in mediump vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat7;
float u_xlat13;
float u_xlat18;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat7;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat7);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat3.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_2.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_2.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat3.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat3.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_2.w + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.yyy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_37)) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_0.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_38 = max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_38 = min(u_xlat16_38, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_38) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_17.xy = u_xlat16_6.xx * u_xlat16_6.xx + vec2(1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_17.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_17.xxx;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_36 * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) + (-u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_36);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_36 = min(max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_36 = clamp(u_xlat16_36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_17.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_38 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_38 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat16_4.x = exp2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat11.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = min(u_xlat16_7.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = max(u_xlat16_7.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_36 = (-u_xlat0.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_36 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_37 / u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_14 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_14 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_14 * u_xlat16_3.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_3.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_3.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xxx;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy;
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(_FurLengthTex, u_xlat16_0.xy, 0.0).x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.446999997, 0.446999997, 0.446999997);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);

    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_17.y + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;

    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_12.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));

    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_12.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_1.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_34 = (-_SelfShadowStrength) * 0.552999973 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;

    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;

    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);

    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;

    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;

    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);

    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;

    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_17;
bool u_xlatb22;
mediump float u_xlat16_23;

mediump float u_xlat16_34;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = texture(_FurLengthTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.x + -0.00999999978;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat0.x);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat0.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0.x = texture(_NoiseTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);

    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.xy = u_xlat16_12.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_15.xxx;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat16_12.yyy;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy;
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(_FurLengthTex, u_xlat16_0.xy, 0.0).x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.632000029, 0.632000029, 0.632000029);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat11.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_12.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_1.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_34 = (-_SelfShadowStrength) * 0.156000018 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_34) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.874000013, 0.874000013, 0.874000013);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

{

#else

    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;

    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_17.y + 1.0;

    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in mediump vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in mediump vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in mediump vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
bool u_xlatb1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat15;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy;
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(_FurLengthTex, u_xlat16_0.xy, 0.0).x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(0.874000013, 0.874000013, 0.874000013);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _NoiseTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
bool u_xlatb11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_17;
bool u_xlatb22;
mediump float u_xlat16_23;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_34;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = texture(_FurLengthTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.x + -0.00999999978;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat0.x);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat0.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0.x = texture(_NoiseTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.xy = u_xlat16_12.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_15.xxx;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat16_12.yyy;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_15.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5.x = clamp(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_5.x + -0.0990760028;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_5.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * _AlphaAdjust;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 1.29198968;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_0;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat15;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy;
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(_FurLengthTex, u_xlat16_0.xy, 0.0).x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat16_4.x = exp2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat11.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vs_TEXCOORD8.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_12.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_1.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in mediump vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in mediump vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in mediump vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
bool u_xlatb1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat15;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy;
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(_FurLengthTex, u_xlat16_0.xy, 0.0).x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in mediump vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in mediump vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in mediump vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
bool u_xlatb1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat15;
float u_xlat22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _NoiseTex_ST.xy + _NoiseTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy;
    u_xlat1.x = textureLod(_FurLengthTex, u_xlat16_0.xy, 0.0).x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = max(u_xlat8.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat8.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat15 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat15;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = max(u_xlat2.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_3.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_3.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(_FurLength);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + in_POSITION0.xyz;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat1.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = (u_xlatb1) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat8.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat8.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat8.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat22 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat22 = max(u_xlat22, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat22);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat22) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD5.w = u_xlat4.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat16_10.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-_MainlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.y = (-_AddlightAttenuation);
    u_xlat16_6.z = (-_RimlightAttenuation);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position = (-u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_3.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _NoiseTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _FurLengthTex;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = texture(_FurLengthTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat0.x + -0.00999999978;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.00999999978>=u_xlat0.x);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.00999999978>=u_xlat0.x;
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : 0.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_0.x = texture(_NoiseTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw).x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_12.xy = u_xlat16_12.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_15.xxx;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat16_12.yyy;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.zzz * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_15.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5.x = clamp(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_5.x + -0.299236;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_5.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * _AlphaAdjust;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * 1.11856818;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x + -0.0500000007;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * (-u_xlat16_1.xxx) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

    u_xlat16_16.x = max(u_xlat16_16.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_16.x = log2(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_16.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_16.x = exp2(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_16.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;

    u_xlat16_17.xy = u_xlat16_6.xx * u_xlat16_6.xx + vec2(1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x * u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_4.x * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_39;

    u_xlat16_4.x = exp2(u_xlat16_4.x);

    u_xlat16_7.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat0.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_37 + u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_5.x / u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(_RimLightDir, _RimLightDir);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_12.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_23 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_23 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_23;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_23 * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = clamp(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_23 = u_xlat16_12.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_23;
    u_xlat16_23 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_23 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = min(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1

#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BaseMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BaseColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmissionColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _BumpScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OcclusionStrength;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_BaseMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
